Total Profit](https://teespring.leankit.com/Boards/View/118961411/191251240)\r\n[Leankit 8e) Keen wrapper for cancelled orders and units](https://teespring.leankit.com/Boards/View/118961411/192010913)\r\n\r\nThis is a wrapper around the `keen` gem to get the analytics. A couple of things to note:\r\n\r\n1) Right now I'm using `campaign_ids` instead of `campaign_root_id`. Originally when @novito and I talked, using `campaign_ids` for our keen queries would allow us to get past history. However, after talking w/ @emilyyidan, we can probably go the much easier route and pass in `campaign_root_id` and not care if we have missing data (it'd be more like we're 0s).\r\n\r\n2) I'm using `vcr` to record the actual API requests made from keen to help w/ testing. The APIs are calling against the `Teespring-Staging` keen project. I've added a filter to remove the Keen keys from the recorded APIs. This should help w/ testing.\r\n\r\nWould love everyone's feedback!",

    "body": "Leankit: https://teespring.leankit.com/Boards/View/118961411/196137288\r\n\r\n**PROBLEM**\r\nSome campaigns show up in search even though they are suspended. This is because the algolia search indices for those campaigns are out of sync w/ the models. When campaigns are suspended, algolia *should* correctly update the index, but it seems that sometimes it doesn't.\r\n\r\n**SOLUTION**\r\nRun an automated rake task daily that manually reindexes campaigns suspended w/in the last day. This will ensure that the campaigns that are somehow out of sync with algolia are kept in sync.\r\n\r\n**QA**\r\nCreate some campaigns and make sure they show up in search. I'll manually suspend some w/o updating their algolia indices (if I change the campaign_state_id manually in the database, algolia-rails won't know to update the index). Once you confirm that the suspended campaigns are still showing up in search, I'll run the worker and you can confirm that they no longer show up in search results.",

    "body": "### Problem\r\n\r\nNow that the `orders` table is UTF-8 encoded we need make sure that all of the other tables that have a `email_hash` field are also in UTF-8.  The reason being is if we were to ever join on that email, the join wouldn't work properly and our DB collapses.\r\n\r\n### Solution\r\n\r\nMigrate the tables that are in latin1 that have a `email_hash` column to UTF-8.\r\n\r\n### QA Instructions\r\n\r\n1. Nothing to QA\r\n\r\n### When to merge\r\n\r\nWe're going to merge / deploy this Monday night when there aren't a lot of people on the site. It will be the same time that we run the long `campaigns` table migration.  ",

    "body": "### Problem\r\n\r\nWe are losing money on DTG printing when a campaign has two sided prints.\r\n\r\n### Solution\r\n\r\nWhen a campaign is going to DTG and has artwork on both sides of the garment, add $3.00 to the campaign's base price. The total base price will be $12.00 at that point.\r\n\r\n### QA Instructions\r\n\r\n1. Go to the composer and create a campaign with artwork ONLY on the front\r\n1. Go to Step 2, and change the goal to < 10 (DTG realm). Note the base price at this time.\r\n1. Go back to Step 1 and add artwork to the back of the shirt\r\n1. The base price should increase by $3.00\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n1. Launch a campaign with a colored \"Hanes Tagless Tee\" selling for $20.25 with art on the front and back\r\n1. Buy three of these shirts\r\n1. End the campaign\r\n1. The total profit given to the seller should be $6.00\r\n\r\n\r\n### Side Note\r\n\r\nI think should be used as an example on how to pull logic out of `app/models/campaign.rb`. If we all remove 50-60 LOC every PR that file will get whittled down to nothing soon!",

    },
    "body": "[Leankit](https://teespring.leankit.com/Boards/View/118961411/194954440)\r\n\r\nWhen fetching the unique orders (by email) within an audience that a seller could send their emails to, we were using ```.group``` and ```.find_each```. As a consequence some of the buyers would get more than one email. This is because ```find_each``` overwrites the purpose of ```group``` and make it return duplicated rows. Example for audience 1209:\r\n\r\n```\r\nirb(main):001:0> audience = Audience.find(1209)\r\nirb(main):002:0> eligible_campaigns = audience.eligible_campaigns\r\nirb(main):003:0> eoq = EmailableOrdersQuery.new(eligible_campaigns)\r\nirb(main):004:0> all_orders = eoq.get_all\r\nirb(main):005:0> all_orders.size\r\n=> 4009 # These are orders with unique emails.\r\n# Now let's see what ```find_each``` does\r\nirb(main):006:0> orders_collection = []\r\n=> []\r\nirb(main):007:0> all_orders.find_each { |o| orders_collection << o.email }\r\nirb(main):009:0> orders_collection.size\r\n=> 5009 \r\nirb(main):012:0> orders_collection.select { |email| email == 'karadmuma@gmail.com' }.size\r\n=> 4\r\n```\r\nThis PR modifies the query class so that we just use ```group by orders.email_hash``` and the interactor iterates over the records with ```each```.\r\n\r\n@ekosz @rrzein Could you take a look please? \r\n\r\n**QA instructions**\r\n\r\n- As a seller you should be able to send emails to your audiences.\r\n- As a buyer you should not receive the email more than once if you have purchased from a campaign more than once, or if you have purchased from different campaigns that are in the same audience.",

(Did not change the width of input box as it will break the UI )\r\n\r\n## Steps to Reproduce: \r\n1) Go to Password Recovery Page on the site.\r\n2) Select Deutsch or Francais language from the language dropdown.\r\n3) You will observe that the email-id placeholder is not fitting inside the input box\r\n\r\n## Before Fix:\r\n![before_fix](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/10937997/7406903/640eeef0-ef28-11e4-8112-590b1927f699.png)\r\n\r\n## After Fix:\r\n![after_fix](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/10937997/7406904/6cd65618-ef28-11e4-9624-95dcb8e6ea78.png)\r\n\r\n@goodgravy  @azer @johannesma \r\n\r\n\r\n",

      "starred_url": "https://api.github.com/users/ekosz/starred{/owner}{/repo}",
      "subscriptions_url": "https://api.github.com/users/ekosz/subscriptions",

    },
    "body": "### Problem \r\n\r\nWe need to update domestic shipping rates on the site from $3.85 + $1.00 to $3.99 + $2.00. The current shipping rates cache made makes this a very difficult to change. The problem right now is that when we update the rates, the current cache won't expire for 24 hours. Thats 24 hours where users will see $3.85 on checkout, but charged $3.99 when they finish.\r\n\r\n### Solution\r\n\r\nRemove the public `Cache-Control`, and replace it with a public `Etag` that is very fast to verify. The new flow looks like this.\r\n\r\n1. The very first time a shipping rate is requested for a campaign:\r\n  1. It finds the rate\r\n  1. Generates an `Etag` composed of the campaign's region and the most recent shipping rate `updated_at`\r\n  1. Returns the rates\r\n1. Every other request to the shipping rates will:\r\n  1. Check if the campaign's region or most recent shipping rate changed\r\n  1. If NOT return the old rates (without spending time looking them up)\r\n  1. If SO Repeat step 1\r\n\r\nThis keeps the request still very fast and cached (only performing 3 SQL calls), but invalidates itself when the rates update.  This is a good example where we create a compromise between speed and dymacy.\r\n\r\n### QA Instructions\r\n\r\n1. Visit a checkout page and note the shipping rate\r\n1. Refresh the page, you should see the same shipping rate\r\n1. Ask Eric to update the shipping rates for staging\r\n1. Refresh the page, you should see the new shipping rate\r\n1. Finish checkout, you should have been charged the new shipping rate",
